generic
binary_auto
Second Sequence Number / Alpha Window Threshold
"Set control point rotation" pre-emission operator now correctly produces right-handed matrices [previously it would produce left-handed ones].
"Position within sphere random" no longer supports the "randomly distribute to highest supplied Control Point" feature\n\t"Emit continuously" and "Emit noise" no longer support "scale emission to used control points".\n\t"Position from control points" had a max control point added to it.
"Twist around axis" force now rotates around the specified control point instead of control point 0.\n
"Remap control point orientation to rotation" rewritten to make more sense.\n
Made disabling operators + children actually fully work.\n
Particle initializers always run. Previously, some initializers would silently be skipped.\n
"Remap control point orientation to rotation" does something approaching sanity for the cases I looked at.  If we have cases where this isn't appropriate, we can split out the behavior.\n
Fixed bugs in "Position along path sequential" where it could incorrectly create too many particles at the last control point. Also fixed issues with control points specified in backward order in that operator as well as "Movement lock to saved position along path".\n
Fixed "Inherit Attribute from Parent Particles" not keeping parent particles in sync with children.\n
Fixed "Animation Type" in Sprite Renderer not working for non-particle normal alignment types.\n
Ropes and Trails now properly use visibility settings for radius and alpha - previously settings here were ignored so systems which have this set will begin working on update.  Double-check your Rope/Trail Visibility Inputs.\n
Fixed Float Evaluator "Particle Count Percent of Total Count" being off-by-one at the end. Double-check remapping of any Particle Count Normalized float evaluators.\n
